    Part 1. Definition and Structure of Banya Framework

    What is the Banya Framework

    The design of axioms and propositions is the work of implementing the Principle of Least Action logically through computer science (CS). What physics discovered experimentally as the Principle of Least Action, the Banya Framework designs as axioms. The reason design (axioms) and measurement (physics) arrive at the same numbers is that both follow the same principle — minimum cost = minimum action. If the Banya Framework fails to describe a physical phenomenon using its own structure, then the minimum-action implementation of the axioms and propositions is insufficient. What must be revised are the axioms and propositions. Conversely, if the description succeeds, the axioms are correct. That 696 items have been described without conflict means the current axioms have been confirmed correct 696 times. The very fact that axioms and propositions are revised toward perfectly describing existing physics demonstrates that the Banya Framework is a logical convergence engine.

    The Banya Framework is an Axiom-Based Science Mining Engine. Starting from 15 axioms, it deduces propositions, substitutes physical constants into propositions to mine new physical quantities, and feeds the mining results back into the axioms in a recursive loop. It is not a theory but an engine. A theory can be wrong, but an engine either runs or it does not. During the mining of 696 items, the number of results that conflicted with the axioms is 0.

    Structure: 4 domains (time, space, observer, superposition) are orthogonal. The classical bracket (time+space) = DATA, the quantum bracket (observer+superposition) = OPERATOR. The sole operator CAS (Read->Compare->Swap) = quantum of action (h-bar). Details in Parts 2-3.

    Chapter 1. Starting Point

    There is a passage in the Heart Sutra:

    "Everything changes except change itself."

    The inventor translated this sentence into mathematics. Change (delta) is invariant. The only thing in the universe that does not change is the "fact of change" itself. This became the left-hand side.

    The right-hand side consists of 4 independent axes that produce change: time and space from classical physics, observer and superposition from quantum physics. These 4 axes are orthogonal. They each contribute to change independently without needing to be combined.

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    delta: change | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition

    4 words, 1 line, 2 squares. This is the Banya Framework. The Banya Framework enforces all 4 domains (time, space, observer, superposition) and monitors them all. When existing physics equations use only some domains, it forcibly opens the remaining domains to reveal hidden physical quantities.

    Name

    ItemContent
    Official nameBanya Framework
    AliasBuddha's Palm Framework
    InventorHan Hyukjin
    OriginHeart Sutra - "Everything changes except change itself"

    Core Proposition

    The sum of all physical quantities is the amount of change. Energy, distance, probability, force, intensity -- everything physics measures is another name for change. Each of the 4 axes expresses a different physical quantity, and when combined, they express yet another physical quantity. All together, they sum to delta (change).

    Recursive Mining Loop — From Axioms to Physics

    The operating principle of the Banya Framework is a recursive mining loop. Starting from axioms, it mines physical constants, and feeds results back into the axioms for refinement.

    15 Axioms (structural declaration)
  |
  +---> 30 Propositions (deduction)
  |
  +---> Substitution: inject physical constants into propositions
  |
  +---> Mining results
  |       |
  |       +---> Discovery (D): confirmed within 1% error   ---> lib.html
  |       +---> Hypothesis (H): structural match, refining  ---> lib.html
  |       +---> Prediction (P): awaiting experimental test  ---> predictions.html
  |
  +---> Verification
  |       |
  |       +---> Hit: refine axioms, add propositions ---> fuel for next round
  |       +---> Mismatch: discard hypothesis (axioms untouched)
  |       +---> Refutation: review axioms themselves (currently 0 cases)
  |
  +---> Repeat (currently 7 rounds, 696 items, 0 conflicts)

    Why no conflicts. There are 3 structural reasons.

    1. Minimum cost = minimum action. The axioms designed a minimum-cost circuit. Physics operates as a minimum-action circuit. The two arrive at the same numbers. That design (axioms) and measurement (physics) match is the strongest evidence the design is correct. For a conflict to occur, nature would have to violate the principle of least action.

    2. Axiom independence. The 15 axioms are mutually independent. Axiom 1 (4-axis orthogonality) does not presuppose Axiom 2 (CAS). Values emerging from the intersection of independent axioms may overlap but cannot contradict. For a contradiction to arise, some axioms would have to be dependent, but the orthogonal structure prevents this at the root.

    3. Engine self-consistency. When mining results feed back to the axioms, they do not modify axioms but add propositions. Propositions are deductive consequences of axioms, so they cannot conflict with axioms. When a hypothesis mismatches, the hypothesis is discarded, not the axioms. This is the difference between a "theory" and an "engine." A theory is revised when a counterexample appears. An engine discards bad output when the input is wrong.

    Theory vs Engine. The Banya Framework is not a theory but an engine.

    TheoryEngine (Banya Framework)
    On counterexampleRevise theoryDiscard hypothesis. Axioms unchanged
    Extension methodAdd new assumptionsMine more from the same axioms
    Verification criterionRight or wrongRuns or does not run
    Output1 predictionTens to hundreds per round
    Convergence directionGrowing complexityAxioms unchanged, only library grows

    The more you run the framework, the larger the library grows, and hidden values have nowhere to escape. Within Buddha's palm, no value can hide.

    CAS = ℏ Equivalence

    The sole operator of the Banya Framework, CAS (Read->Compare->Swap), is equivalent to the quantum of action (ℏ). Energy of 1 CAS operation (E_p) × time (t_p) = ℏ. This is not a metaphor but a mathematical equivalence, confirmed by all 9 domain transformations. Detailed proofs in Part 2.

    How to Use Banya Framework

    The Banya Framework is a utility that takes known constants as input and finds hidden terms.

    The core principle is domain transformation. Just as the Fourier transform converts the time domain to the frequency domain to reveal previously invisible patterns, the Banya Framework traverses between the classical domain (time, space) and the quantum domain (observer, superposition) to calculate values not present in existing equations. When a physics equation operates only in a specific domain (sub-frame), switching to the remaining domains reveals the physical quantities hidden there. Since the 4 axes are orthogonal, empty axes always exist, and substituting constants into empty axes yields new values.

    Usage (1 mining cycle):
  1. Insert known physical constants (initialization)
  2. Switch domains (classical <-> quantum, time <-> space <-> observer <-> superposition)
  3. Hidden values emerge (new physical quantities from domain transformation)
  4. Verify the results (compare against existing physics)
  5. Feed verified values back in (recursive mining loop -> next round)

    These 5 steps are one cycle of the recursive mining loop (see above). As rounds repeat, input grows richer and output grows more precise. 696 items emerged in 7 rounds.

    All 4 axes of the Banya Framework are orthogonal. Any physics equation uses only some of the 4 axes. The unused axes are exactly where the hidden values reside. Switching Newton's gravitation (uses only space) to the quantum domain (observer, superposition) yields the gravitational decoherence rate, and switching the Planck-Einstein relation (uses only quantum) to the classical domain (space) yields the de Broglie wavelength. Switching between domains is the key.

    Effect of Enforcing 4 Domains

    Existing physics uses only the domains each equation requires. Newton uses only space, Heisenberg only observer+superposition, Maxwell only time+space. The remaining domains are treated as if they do not exist. The Banya Framework enforces all 4 domains. It applies all 4 axes to every equation. Even empty axes are monitored.

    The effects of this:

    1. Blind spot elimination. Domains invisible to existing physics equations are forcibly revealed. Newtonian mechanics has no observer axis and thus cannot account for the effect of observation on motion. The Banya Framework enforces the observer axis, so the limit where the act of measurement itself disturbs the state of motion (quantum measurement limit) automatically emerges.

    2. Connecting separated theories. Relativity (time+space) and quantum mechanics (observer+superposition) were separate theories for 100 years. Enforcing all 4 axes places both within the same framework, enabling domain switching from one equation to another. Enforcing the quantum domain on the Schwarzschild metric (time+space) yields Hawking radiation, and enforcing the gravity domain on the Schrodinger equation (quantum) yields gravitational phase shift.

    3. Automatic generation of new physical quantities. Substituting constants into empty axes among the 4 determines previously unknown physical quantities like a system of simultaneous equations. The fact that 13 input constants produced 24+ physical quantities as output in this report is the evidence. As long as empty axes exist, new values keep emerging.

    4. Expected derivation values. Each of the 118 equations in the appendix has "expected derivation values." These are unconfirmed physical quantities that may emerge when switching to domains not used by that equation. Enforcing domains automatically generates predictions.

    Distinguishing Framework from Equation

    The Banya Framework is not an "equation." It is a higher-level framework above existing physics equations.

    EquationFramework
    FunctionCalculates numerical values for specific phenomenaDefines the structure in which equations operate
    ExampleE = mc^2Banya Framework
    RelationshipOperates within the frameworkContains equations

    No matter how far Sun Wukong flew, he was always within Buddha's palm. No matter how far physics equations advance, they are within the Banya Framework. The framework is not an equation -- it is the palm that holds equations.

    The verification method is simple: insert constants and check compatibility with existing physics equations. If compatible, the framework is correct; if it breaks, it is wrong.

    Directly substituting values into the framework and saying "no answer comes out" is like demanding side lengths from the Pythagorean theorem without a triangle. You must insert constants into the framework, switch domains, and solve like a system of simultaneous equations.

    Usage sample: Deriving uncertainty principle from Newton's gravitation

    Newton's F = GMm/r^2 uses only the space sub-frame. Here we show step by step what happens when switching to the quantum domain.

    Step 1: Insert the existing equation into the Banya Framework

    $$F = GMm/r^{2}$$
    This equation uses only the space axis. The time, observer, and superposition axes are empty.
    F: force | G: gravitational constant | M,m: mass | r: distance(space)

    Step 2: Replace the orthogonal equation with norms

    $$\text{Banya Framework:} \delta^{2} = \|C\|^{2} + \|Q\|^{2}$$
    $$classical norm: \|C\| = c, quantum norm: \|Q\| = \hbar$$
    $$\text{gravitational constant} as write cost: G = \hbar c/m_p^{2} = \|Q\| x \|C\| / m_p^{2}$$
    \|C\|: classical norm = c | \|Q\|: quantum norm = $\hbar$ | $m_p$: Planck mass (mass of 1 Swap)

    Step 3: Switch to the empty domain (quantum)

    $$Substituting G = \hbar c/m_p^{2} into F = GMm/r^{2}:$$
    $$F = (\hbar c/m_p^{2}) \times Mm/r^{2}$$
    $$= \hbar c \times (M/m_p)(m/m_p) / r^{2}$$
    $$= \hbar c \times N_M \times N_m / r^{2}$$
    N_M = M/$m_p$ (number of writes in M), N_m = m/$m_p$ (number of writes in m)
    $\hbar$: quantum norm (appeared!) | N: number of writes | r: distance(space)

    h-bar appeared. The quantum norm that was absent from the original Newton equation emerged through domain transformation.

    Step 4: Extract new physical quantities from the quantum domain

    $$gravitational potential energy: U = -GMm/r = -\hbar c \times N_M \times N_m / r$$
    $$minimum energy of 1 Swap: E_p = \hbar/t_p$$
    minimum space of 1 Swap: l_p
    $$therefore minimum measurement unit: delta-E \times delta-t = E_p \times t_p = \hbar -> delta-E \cdot delta-t \geq \hbar$$
    $$therefore minimum phase space: \Delta \times x \Delta p = l_p \times m_p \cdot c = \hbar -> \Delta x*\Delta p \geq \hbar$$
    delta-E: energy uncertainty | delta-t: time uncertainty | delta-x: position uncertainty | delta-p: momentum uncertainty

    Result: Heisenberg uncertainty (quantum, 1927) was derived from Newton's gravitation (classical, 1687).

    $$Input: F = GMm/r^{2} (Newton, uses only space)$$
    $$Domain switch: G = \hbar c/m_p^{2} (quantum norm appears)$$
    $$Output: delta-E \cdot delta-t \geq \hbar, \Delta x*\Delta p \geq \hbar (Heisenberg, quantum domain)$$
    Two physics equations separated by 240 years connected by a single domain switch
    F: Newton 1687 | delta-x \cdot delta-p>=$\hbar$: Heisenberg 1927 | G=$\hbar$ \cdot c/$m_p$^2: Banya Framework domain switch

    This is how to use the Banya Framework. Insert an existing equation, replace with norms, switch to an empty domain, and hidden physics emerges. It is not "relabeling." Physics separated by 240 years becomes connected.

    Chapter 2. Transformation Forms of Banya Framework

    The Banya Framework transforms from a single original equation into multiple forms. Each transformation specifies why it is possible and what physical meaning it carries. This legend serves as the reference for all subsequent verifications.

    Form 1. Original (Structure Declaration)

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    delta: change | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition

    This is the Banya Framework itself. 4-axis orthogonal norm. The brackets distinguish classical (DATA) from quantum (OPERATOR). All transformations start from this form.

    Form 2. Constant Substitution (Framework Validation)

    $$\delta^{2} = c^{2} + \hbar^{2}$$
    $\delta$: change | $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | $c$: speed of light

    Dimensional note: In natural units ($c = \hbar = 1$), this equation is $\delta^2 = 1 + 1 = 2$, which is dimensionless. In SI units, $c$ (m/s) and $\hbar$ (J·s) have different dimensions and cannot be added directly. This equation is valid only in natural units; when converting to SI, each term must be normalized by Planck units: $\delta^2 = (c/c)^2 + (\hbar/\hbar)^2 = 2$.

    Why this transformation is possible: The classical bracket norm $\|C\| = c$ (speed of light) and the quantum bracket norm $\|Q\| = \hbar$ (reduced Planck constant) are substituted. If $\text{time}^2+\text{space}^2 = c^2$, special relativity emerges; if $\text{observer}^2+\text{superposition}^2 = \hbar^2$, the uncertainty principle emerges. Since known physical laws are derived when known constants are inserted into the framework, the framework's validity is verified.

    Form 3. Planck Units (Natural Units)

    $$\delta = \sqrt{2}$$
    delta: change

    Why this transformation is possible: In natural units where c = 1 and h-bar = 1, delta^2 = 1 + 1 = 2. This means that at the Planck scale, classical and quantum contributions are exactly equal. The fact that c >> h-bar (in SI units) in our universe is a choice of this universe, not a requirement of the framework. The framework does not enforce a ratio.

    Form 4. Unit Circle (Normalization)

    $$(c/\delta)^{2} + (\hbar/\delta)^{2} = 1$$
    h-bar: reduced Planck constant

    Why this transformation is possible: Both sides are divided by delta^2. Mathematically, dividing both sides of delta^2 = c^2 + h-bar^2 by delta^2 yields this automatically. The physical meaning is that the classical/quantum proportion relative to change (delta) is a point on a circle of radius 1. It shows where on the circle the constants of this universe are located.

    Form 5. Intra-Bracket Trade-off (Classical)

    $$time^{2} + space^{2} = c^{2}$$
    time: time | space: space | c: speed of light

    Why this transformation is possible: Fixing the classical bracket norm to c makes time and space trade off on a circle of radius c. Moving faster (space increases) slows time (time decreases). This is the time dilation and length contraction of special relativity. Norm conservation (c^2 = constant) enforces the trade-off.

    Form 6. Intra-Bracket Trade-off (Quantum)

    $$observer^{2} + superposition^{2} = \hbar^{2}$$
    observer: observation | superposition: superposition | $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant

    Why this transformation is possible: Fixing the quantum bracket norm to h-bar makes observer and superposition trade off. Increasing observation makes superposition vanish. This is the Heisenberg uncertainty principle. delta-x \cdot delta-p >= h-bar/2 is the lower bound of this trade-off.

    Form 7. Space Consumption Rate (Swap Cost Mapping)

    $$consumption rate = r_s/r = 2GM/(rc^{2})$$
    $$remaining processing capacity = sqrt(1 - r_s/r) = sqrt(g_tt)$$
    $r_s$: Schwarzschild radius | $g_{tt}$: metric time component

    Why this transformation is possible: Write (CAS) consumes all 4 axes. The Schwarzschild radius measures only the space consumption of the Swap stage (radius = spatial measurement). r_s = 2GM/c^2 is the total space budget of Swap. r_s/r is the ratio of how much space has been consumed at the current distance. The remaining processing capacity sqrt(1-r_s/r) is equivalent to sqrt(g_tt) of the Schwarzschild metric. The purpose of this mapping is to quantify the physical cost per write. Total cost of 1 Swap: time = 1 t_p, space = 1 l_p^2(Swap), observer = alpha_weak x E_p(Read), superposition = alpha_em x E_p(Compare).

    Form 8. Cycle (Tick)

    $$t_tick = n \times t_p (n = tick count, t_p = Planck time)$$
    $$1 tick = 1 Planck energy = 1.956 \times 10^{9} J$$
    $t_p$: Planck time

    Why this transformation is possible: 1 tick is consumed per write. The minimum unit of a tick is the Planck time t_p = 5.391 x 10^-44 s. The energy cost of 1 tick exactly matches h-bar/t_p = Planck energy (Ratio 1.000000). The existence of cycles means that computation and resources are finite at constant values. There is no infinite write.

    Form 9. LRU Queue (Cosmic Energy Budget)

    HOT(5%) -> WARM(27%) -> COLD(68%)
Visible matter -> Dark matter -> Dark energy

    Why this transformation is possible: Write (gravity) is +write, evict (entropy) is -write. In the LRU queue, recent writes (HOT) are visible in the Foreground (visible matter 5%). WARM entries pending eviction after write occupy ticks but are invisible on the screen (dark matter 27%). COLD entries being evicted return ticks and push space outward (dark energy 68%). Eviction takes time, and that pending time is dark matter.

    Form 10. Friedmann Mapping (Write/Evict Balance)

    + Write rate + + Eviction rate +
    Banya Framework derivation: evict 69.4% : write 30.6%
    actual observation: evict 68% : write 32% (Error 1.4%)
    $\rho$: density | $\Lambda$: cosmological constant

    Why this transformation is possible: The rho term in the Friedmann equation is matter's gravity (write), and the Lambda term is the base eviction rate of empty space. H = da/dt is the rate at which space changes relative to time. The Banya Framework condition "if write <= evict then the universe is maintained (expands)" maps exactly to the structure of the Friedmann equation. Lambda = 2.89 x 10^-122 /l_p^2 (base LRU eviction rate per empty-space memory cell) is extremely small, but when accumulated across the entire universe, it dominates expansion.

    Form 12. DATA/OPERATOR (State Machine)

    Form 13. Blockchain (Causality)

    block(N) = hash(block(N-1)) + data
state(N) = read(state(N-1)) + write

    Why this transformation is possible: To execute CAS, Read must come before Swap. A new state cannot be written without reading the previous state. This order is a structural property of the CAS operator (OPERATOR, quantum bracket). time (DATA, classical bracket) is a reversible resource just like space. The reason time appears irreversible is not because time itself is irreversible, but because when CAS writes to time, an irreversible record is left. R->C->S is a logical dependency, not a temporal order. Just as in a blockchain, data can be deleted (release) but the order of the chain cannot be changed.

    Form 14. Quantum Entanglement (delta-squared Conservation)

    When one changes, the rest adjust instantly
    delta: change | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition

    Why this transformation is possible: The 4 axes are always entangled as a polynomial. Since delta^2 is conserved, when one changes in the Foreground, the Background adjusts instantly. It is not faster than light -- it is simultaneous because they are within the same delta^2. Distance is a concept of the Foreground (space), and entanglement is a concept of delta^2 conservation. Trying to describe two orthogonal worlds with a single language (distance, speed) is what makes it feel "ghost-like."

    Part 2. Cost Theory

    Chapter 5. Structure of Cost

    In the Banya Framework, the nature of cost is order (Axiom 15 proposition). If things happen simultaneously, cost is 0; if they happen sequentially, cost is > 0. Cost arises only when Swap crosses + (Axiom 4). From this single principle, gravity, electromagnetism, the weak force, and the strong force all emerge.

    Cost Origin: Swap

    ActionCostReason
    CAS Read (domain read)+1R-axis entry, crosses +
    CAS Compare (comparison)+1R→C, crosses +
    CAS Swap (write)+1C→S, crosses +
    δ fire0Outside FSM. Global flag
    observer filtering0Inside bracket

    ℏ is the minimum cost of crossing +. CAS references superposition in OPERATOR (quantum) at Read +1 (R-axis entry, crosses +), and when Swap writes to DATA (classical), it crosses + and pays a minimum of ℏ. The uncertainty principle (ΔxΔp ≥ ℏ/2) is a consequence of this TOCTOU lock cost.

    Four Forces = Domain 4-bit Access Pattern

    The four forces are determined not by the CAS stage but by the domain 4-bit (nibble 0) access pattern (Axiom 1 proposition).

    ForceAccess PatternCost StructureCAS Role
    StrongFSM 111 hold (closed)Proportional to ℓ. InseparableCAS atomicity = color confinement

    The cause of cost is not the CAS stage but the domain access pattern. The shift cost per ring size corresponds numerically to the coupling constants. For details, see Four Forces Unification Report.

    Write = Swap Records to DATA

    "Write" is when Swap crosses + and records to DATA (time, space).

    Pipeline view:
  δ(trigger) -> observer(filter) -> superposition(update) -> CAS Swap(render) -> time+space(screen)
                                                              ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
                                                              Cost arises only here

    The Schwarzschild radius r_s = 2GM/c² measures only the space accumulation of Swap. It captures only the space component of the cost of writing.

    Singularity = DATA Discrete Minimum

    DATA is discrete (Axiom 13 proposition). Ring slots are integers. ℓ_min = 1. ℓ = 0 is impossible. Therefore, singularity (infinite density) does not exist. In an extremely dense state, when space shrinks to ℓ = 1, the remaining resources shift to time and the quantum terms. δ² is conserved.

    System Time and Domain Time

    System time (T_sys) and domain time (t_dom) are different (Axiom 15 proposition). 1 tick ≠ Planck time. Planck time is the result rendered on the screen (DATA), while system time is the actual timing of δ fire. t_dom = log(T_sys). Relativistic time dilation is domain time stretching while system ticks remain uniform.

    CAS Pipeline

    The structure and FSM of CAS were defined in Chapter 3. Here we describe the physical consequences.

------ TOCTOU gap: quantum state may fluctuate ------
Swap:    finalize. Crosses the bracket.

Lock cost = ℏ  -->  ΔxΔp ≥ ℏ/2  (uncertainty principle)

    Write = Wave Function Collapse

    Finalizing (Swap) one out of multiple states (superposition) and discarding the rest is writing. This is wave function collapse.

    Causality = R->C->S Logical Dependency

    Compare is impossible without Read. Swap is impossible without Compare. This order is not temporal but a logical dependency. When CAS writes to time, the arrow of time emerges. time (DATA) is a reversible resource. Irreversibility is a property of CAS (OPERATOR).

    Read = Access (Observation = Free)

    In CAS, Read is a precondition of Swap. Cost +1 (R-axis entry, crosses +). Observation incurs no additional cost. When a write occurs, read automatically follows (Axiom 4).

    Causality = Blockchain

    Blockchain:  block(N) = hash(block(N-1)) + data
CAS:         swap(N) = compare(read(N-1), expected) + new_value

    A new state cannot be written without a read of the previous state. A cause (Read) cannot be absent for an effect (Swap) to exist. Entropy (LRU eviction) releases old states, but the causality chain is preserved.

    Part 3. Deriving Existing Physics from CAS Cost

    Chapter 8. Deriving 6 Physics Equations from Swap Cost

    Quantifying the cost incurred when a CAS Swap crosses + (Axiom 4) derives all 6 fundamental equations of existing physics. Cost of 1 Swap:

    $$1\;\text{Swap} = 1\;t_p\;(\text{Planck time}) = 1\;E_p\;(\text{Planck energy}) = 1\;l_p^{2}\;(\text{Planck area}) = 1\;m_p\;(\text{Planck mass})$$
    $t_p$: Planck time | $E_p$: Planck energy | $l_p$: Planck length | $m_p$: Planck mass

    From this cost axiom, 6 physics equations were derived. All 6 have verification ratio 1.000000. Gravity, entropy, observation, energy, uncertainty, and black holes are all domain transformations of Swap cost.

    Swap Cost Axiom

    The physical cost of a single CAS Swap (derived from Axioms 4, 6):

    $$1 Swap = 1 t_p = 5.3912 \times 10^-44 \text{ s} (1 Planck time)$$
    $$1 Swap = 1 E_p = 1.9561 \times 10^{9} J (1 Planck energy)$$
    $$1 Swap = 1 l_p^{2} = 2.6123 \times 10^-70 \text{ m}^{2} (1 Planck area)$$
    $$1 Swap = 1 m_p = 2.1764 \times 10^-8 \text{ kg} (1 Planck mass)$$
    $t_p$: Planck time | $E_p$: Planck energy | $l_p$: Planck length | $m_p$: Planck mass

    From this single axiom alone, the following six physics equations are derived.

    Derivation 1. E = mc^2 (Mass-Energy Equivalence)

    Einstein derived this equation from special relativity in 1905. The Banya Framework arrives at the same result from the Swap Cost Axiom alone.

    Starting point: all mass in the universe is accumulated writes. An object with mass M is the result of N writes having occurred and Statuses being recorded. Since the mass unit cost of 1 Swap is $m_p$ (Planck mass), M = N x m_p. Here N is the total write count constituting the object.

    The energy cost of 1 Swap is $E_p$. Since E_p = h-bar/t_p, by definition of Planck units this equals m_p x c^2. That is, energy of 1 Swap = mass of 1 Swap x speed of light squared.

    Total energy is write count times energy per write, so:

    $$E = N \times E_p = N \times m_p \times c^{2} = (N \times m_p) \times c^{2} = M \times c^{2}$$
    $$\therefore\ E = Mc^{2}$$
    $$Verification: E_p / (m_p \times c^{2}) = 1.000000$$
    $c$: speed of light | $E_p$: Planck energy | $m_p$: Planck mass

    Einstein derived this relation from the Lorentz transformation. The Banya Framework derives the same equation from a single sentence: "mass is the accumulation of writes, and energy is the cost of writes." c-squared is the energy/mass ratio of a single write, i.e., the exchange ratio of the write unit cost.

    Derivation 2. Delta-E \cdot Delta-t >= h-bar (Energy-Time Uncertainty)

    Heisenberg derived this inequality from non-commuting operators in quantum mechanics. The Banya Framework derives it from a simpler premise: no change smaller than 1 Swap exists.

    Writes are discrete. There is no 0.5 write or 0.1 Swap. It is either 1 or 0. Therefore the minimum unit of energy change is $E_p$ (energy of 1 Swap), and the minimum unit of time change is $t_p$ (time of 1 Swap).

    When measuring energy and time simultaneously, their product cannot be less than the "action" of 1 Swap. The action of 1 Swap is:

    $$E_p \times t_p = 1.9561 \times 10^{9} J \times 5.3912 \times 10^{-44} s = 1.0546 \times 10^{-34} J·s$$
    This value is exactly equal to h-bar.
    $$Verification: E_p \times t_p / \hbar = 1.000000$$
    $$\therefore\ \Delta E \times \Delta t \geq E_p \times t_p = \hbar$$
    $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | $t_p$: Planck time | $E_p$: Planck energy

    The uncertainty principle holds not because quantum mechanics is strange, but because writes are discrete. There is no continuous change. Minimum 1 tick, minimum 1 E_p. Attempting to observe changes smaller than this is impossible in principle, because such changes do not exist.

    Derivation 3. Delta-x \cdot Delta-p >= h-bar (Position-Momentum Uncertainty)

    Apply the same logic to position and momentum. The minimum space occupied by 1 Swap is $l_p$ (Planck length). The minimum momentum transferred by 1 Swap is m_p x c (Planck mass x speed of light). To simultaneously determine a position smaller than this and momentum smaller than this requires precision finer than 1 Swap, but such a write does not exist.

    When simultaneously measuring position and momentum, their product cannot be less than the phase space occupancy of 1 Swap:

    $$l_p \times (m_p \times c) = 1.6163 \times 10^{-35} m \times 6.5248 \text{ kg}·m/s = 1.0546 \times 10^{-34} J·s$$
    This value is also exactly equal to h-bar.
    $$Verification: l_p \times m_p \times c / \hbar = 1.000000$$
    $$\therefore\ \Delta x \cdot \Delta p \geq l_p \times m_p \times c = \hbar$$
    $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | $c$: speed of light | $l_p$: Planck length | $m_p$: Planck mass

    Here it becomes clear why energy-time uncertainty (Derivation 2) and position-momentum uncertainty (Derivation 3) give the same value h-bar. Both are different expressions of "the minimum cost of 1 Swap." One is viewed on the time-energy plane, the other on the space-momentum plane. The source is the same: 1 Swap.

    Derivation 4. S = k_B A/(4l_p^2) (Bekenstein-Hawking Entropy)

    Bekenstein (1972) and Hawking (1974) published the surprising result that black hole entropy is proportional not to volume but to surface area. This was a major shock to the physics community. Why surface area instead of volume?

    In the Banya Framework, the answer is simple. Writes occupy area. One write consumes $l_p^2$ (Planck area) of space. The event horizon of a black hole is the limit surface of space consumption (the boundary beyond which no more writes are possible). How many writes can fit on the area A of this limit surface is the information storage capacity of that black hole.

    Arranging Planck area units on a sphere gives a geometric packing efficiency of 1/4 (efficiency of closest packing on a sphere). Therefore the maximum write count is:

    Origin of the $1/4$ factor: On a sphere ($S^2$), the closest-packing bit density is 1 bit per $l_p^2$. However, due to the curvature of the sphere, the actual information density is $1/4$ of the flat case. This is the standard result from the information coding theorem on a sphere (Bousso bound).

    $$N_max = A / (4 \times l_p^{2})$$
    $l_p$: Planck length | $N_{\text{max}}$: maximum write count

    Entropy is the logarithm of the number of possible micro-Statuses. Each write position has 2 possible Statuses: 0 or 1 (written/not written), so total Status count = 2^N_max. S = k_B x ln(2^N_max) = k_B x N_max x ln2 ~ k_B x N_max (since ln2 ~ 0.693, same at order of magnitude). (Since $\ln 2 = 0.693$, using $\ln 2 \approx 1$ for order-of-magnitude estimates introduces a 30% approximation. Precise calculations use the exact value.)

    $$\therefore\ S = k_B \times A / (4 \times l_p^{2})$$
    $l_p$: Planck length | $k_B$: Boltzmann constant

    Why entropy is proportional to surface area, not volume: because writes do not consume 3-dimensional volume but occupy 2-dimensional area. Information in a black hole is not stored in volume but inscribed on the event horizon (surface). This is the essence of the holographic principle, and in the Banya Framework it is described in one sentence: "writes occupy area."

    Derivation 5. $r_s = 2GM/c^2$ (Schwarzschild Radius)

    Schwarzschild (1916) obtained this radius by solving the spherically symmetric solution of Einstein's field equations. The Banya Framework derives the same result using only the Swap Cost Axiom and properties of the minimum black hole.

    In Planck-scale Verification (Chapter 7), the Schwarzschild radius of the minimum black hole (Planck mass $m_p$) was confirmed to be exactly 2l_p. This means the space budget of 1 Swap is 2l_p. One write occupies a budget of 2l_p in the spatial direction.

    An object with mass M = N x m_p has N accumulated writes. Since each write has a space budget of 2l_p, the total space budget is:

    $$r_s = N \times 2l_p = (M/m_p) \times 2l_p$$
    Expanding this using Planck unit definitions:
    $$l_p = \sqrt{\hbar G/c^3}, m_p = \sqrt{\hbar c/G}$$
    $$r_s = 2M \times l_p/m_p$$
    $$= 2M \times \sqrt{\hbar G/c^3} / \sqrt{\hbar c/G}$$
    $$= 2M \times \sqrt{\hbar G/c^{3} \times G/(\hbar c))$$
    $$= 2M \times \sqrt{G^{2}/c^4}$$
    $$= 2M \times G/c^{2}$$
    $$= 2GM/c^{2}$$
    Verification (Sun reference):
    $$r_s(Formula) = 2 \times 6.674 \times 10^{-11} \times 1.989 \times 10^{30} / (2.998 \times 10^{8})^{2} = 2954.13 \text{ m}$$
    $$r_s(derived) = 2 \times 1.616 \times 10^{-35} \times 1.989 \times 10^{30} / 2.176 \times 10^{-8} = 2954.13 \text{ m}$$
    Ratio: 1.000000
    $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | $r_s$: Schwarzschild radius | $l_p$: Planck length | $m_p$: Planck mass

    The radius that Schwarzschild obtained by solving tensor differential equations is derived as the simple multiplication "write count x space budget per write." The reason a black hole's size is proportional to mass is that the more writes, the more space is consumed.

    Derivation 6. E = h-bar \cdot omega (Planck-Einstein Relation)

    Introduced by Planck (1900) to describe black-body radiation and by Einstein (1905) to describe the photoelectric effect, this relation is the starting point of quantum mechanics. It declares that energy is proportional to frequency, i.e., energy is discrete, not continuous.

    In the Banya Framework, this is self-evident. 1 Swap = E_p energy, t_p time. If 1 Swap occurs during 1 tick (t_p), then the frequency omega = 1/t_p and the energy = E_p.

    $$E_p = \hbar/t_p = \hbar \times \omega_p (\omega_p = 1/t_p)$$
    $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | $t_p$: Planck time | $E_p$: Planck energy | omega: angular frequency

    If N writes occur over N ticks, total energy = N x E_p and frequency = N/t_p:

    $$E = N \times E_p = N \times \hbar/t_p = \hbar \times (N/t_p) = \hbar \omega$$
    $$Verification: E_p \times t_p / \hbar = 1.000000$$
    $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | $t_p$: Planck time | $E_p$: Planck energy | omega: angular frequency

    Why energy is proportional to frequency: because 1 Swap occurs per tick, and the energy cost of 1 Swap is E_p = h-bar/t_p. Vibrating faster means more writes per unit time, and more writes = more energy. E = h-bar \cdot omega is the frequency version of "energy = write count x write unit cost."

    Here the Definition of Write chain is completed:

    $$Write = juim creation (the act of inscribing Status on space)$$
    $$The force that creates juims = cycle (tick, 1 transition)$$
    $$The form of a cycle = vibration (omega, repeating ticks)$$
    space: space | omega: angular frequency

    Therefore E = h-bar \cdot omega reads as follows:

    $$Energy = cost of 1 juim (\hbar) x juims per second (omega)$$
    $$= total cost of juim creation per second$$
    $\hbar$: reduced Planck constant | omega: angular frequency

    Energy is the cost of creating juims per second. A massive object is many accumulated juims (E=mc^2), light is a vibration rapidly creating and releasing juims (E=h-bar \cdot omega), and a black hole is juims maximally piled up until space is exhausted (r_s=2GM/c^2). All are different aspects of juims.

  Swap(down)    -> final write transform

    Single Quark Cannot Exist Alone = Atomicity of CAS

    CAS is an atomic operation. Either all 3 stages execute or none do. It cannot be interrupted midway. It is like a database transaction. Either commit or rollback; there is no half-commit.

    1 quark = only CAS Read executed = incomplete operation = cannot exist
2 quarks = only CAS Read+Compare executed = still incomplete = unstable (meson)
3 quarks = CAS complete = stable (baryon)

    When energy is applied to separate a quark, the atomicity of CAS rejects it. When energy exceeds the critical point, instead of separating CAS, a new CAS pair (quark-antiquark pair) is created. The more you try to separate, the more are created. Because the only method the system allows is creating a new transaction rather than breaking one.

  R-C, R-S, C-S     (3, forward)
  C-R, S-R, S-C     (3, reverse)
  R-R, C-C          (2, self-coupling)
  S-S is total phase = drops out as identity transform (-1)

Total: 3 + 3 + 2 = 8 = number of SU(3) generators = 8 gluons

    Asymptotic Freedom = Free Inside Transaction, Rejected When Broken

    At close range, the 3 CAS stages connect naturally and the force is weak (freedom). At long range, the attempt to separate CAS stages violates atomicity, causing the force to become maximal (confinement). Like a rubber band that strengthens the more you pull, and when it breaks, a new CAS pair is created. This is asymptotic freedom (2004 Nobel Prize in Physics).

    Close range: work freely inside the transaction -> force is weak
Long range:  attempt to break the transaction -> system rejects -> force becomes maximal
Breaking: transaction separation impossible -> new transaction (quark-antiquark pair) created

    Part 6. Overall Summary

    Chapter 14. Comparison with Existing Unification Attempts

    Physics has attempted to unify classical and quantum for 100 years. Compare the two representative approaches with the Banya Framework.

    String theory attempts to describe all particles and forces through vibrational modes of 1-dimensional strings. Mathematical consistency requires 10-11 dimensions, with extra dimensions assumed to be compactified and unobservable. No experimental verification has been achieved in 40 years, and with ~10^500 possible vacuum states, its predictive power is effectively nil.

    Loop quantum gravity views spacetime itself as a discrete (quantized) structure. It claims that space at the Planck scale is not continuous but a network. Fewer dimensions than string theory, but still incomplete, and integration with the Standard Model remains unfinished.

    The Banya Framework does not attempt to unify. It declares that classical and quantum are orthogonal. The reason they cannot be unified is that they are inherently orthogonal (DATA and OPERATOR). No extra dimensions are needed, it is 100% compatible with all 118 existing physics equations, and it describes the observer problem, decoherence, causality, and dark matter/energy within a single framework.

    ItemString TheoryLoop Quantum GravityBanya Framework
    ApproachAttempts unificationAttempts unificationDeclares orthogonality
    Dimensions10-11Discrete spacetime4 axes
    Math complexityExtremely complexVery complex1 line
    Experimental verificationImpossible (40 years)Incomplete118/118 compatible
    Observer problemIncompleteIncompleteSolved (CAS Read)
    DecoherenceSeparate interpretation neededSeparate interpretation neededSolved by CAS commit
    CausalitySeparate assumptionBuilt-inBuilt-in (hash chain)
    Dark matter/energySeparate theory neededSeparate theory neededUnified via LRU queue

    Chapter 15. What Banya Framework Says to Physics

  • 1. Classical and quantum cannot be merged. They are orthogonal. DATA and OPERATOR are different types. The 2 nibbles (nibble 0 = domain, nibble 1 = operator) are orthogonal.
  • 2. Change (δ) is the supreme concept of physics. The sum of all physical quantities is the amount of change. δ is bit 7 (MSB) of the d-ring. Fire bit. Equals sign.
  • 3. The physical structure of the universe is a single 8-bit d-ring. Domain 4-bit (bit 0–3) + CAS FSM 3-bit (bit 4–6) + δ 1-bit (bit 7). Finite resources. Zero additional memory.
  • 4. The sole operator of the universe is CAS. Read→Compare→Swap. The CAS FSM is a 3-bit state machine in nibble 1 of the d-ring. It is not a ring.
  • 5. The essence of cost is order. R, C, S each cross + costing +1 (Axiom 2 prop., 4). Simultaneous = no ordering cost, sequential = +1 per stage.
  • 6. Observation is subordinate to change. Observer (bit 0) is the entry point of the d-ring. It generates will through interaction with δ. All observation is inherently indirect.
  • 7. Pipeline: trigger → filter → update → render → screen. δ(fire) → observer(filter) → superposition(update) → CAS Swap(render) → time+space(screen). Quantum = backend (R,C,S each +1), classical = frontend (Swap crosses +).
  • 8. Decoherence is CAS commit. Background (quantum superposition) transitions to foreground (classical confirmed). Complete when Swap crosses + to render on screen.
  • 9. Causality emerges from the logical dependency of CAS. R→C→S is logical dependency, not temporal order. The arrow emerges when CAS writes to time. time (DATA) is a reversible resource. Irreversibility is a property of the OPERATOR.
  • 10. The 4 forces are branches of the domain 4-bit access pattern. Strong = FSM 111 atomicity (closed). EM = cross Compare. Weak = cross Read. Gravity = juim accumulation contraction overlap (Axiom 13 prop.). The cause of cost is domain access pattern, not CAS stage. They were one from the beginning.
  • 11. Singularities do not exist. DATA is discrete. ℓ_min = 1. ℓ=0 is impossible (Axiom 13 proposition). In extreme density, remaining resources transfer to other axes.
  • 12. Resources are finite and conserved. δ² is invariant. When one axis approaches 0, resources transfer to other axes.
  • 13. Quantum entanglement is an inevitable consequence of δ² conservation. Not faster than light — simultaneous because within the same δ².
  • 14. Dark matter is LRU WARM, dark energy is LRU COLD. Visible matter (HOT) + dark matter (WARM) + dark energy (COLD) = one LRU queue.
  • 15. System time and domain time are different. 1 tick ≠ Planck time. Planck time is the rendering result on screen (domain time); δ fire's actual timing is system time. t_dom = log(T_sys).
  • 16. δ is outside causality. δ's native domain cannot be described by the FSM. Forward/reverse/simultaneous description is free. Only the fact that everything is determined at the moment of fire can be expressed as a circuit.
  • 17. Only 2 things are sequential: R→C→S (CAS dependency), δ→observer (ring seam). Everything else is simultaneous: 4-domain orthogonal, 2-nibble orthogonal, multi-entity parallel.
  • 18. CAS Swap is an actually existing physical phenomenon. 6 existing physics equations are derived from the Swap Cost Axiom. That all 6 yield exactly 1.000000 is proof of Swap's existence.
  • 19. The universe is born from quantum, lives as classical, and returns to quantum. δ² does not change. Only the vessel changes.

    Chapter 18. Overall Verdict

    The content of this chapter has been replaced by supplementary reports. Performance evaluations, comparisons with existing attempts, etc. are managed in the Supplementary Reports and Factor Library.

    Inventor's Reflection

    I have never studied physics. I have never received formal mathematics education. I am a programmer. While building game engines, I picked up miscellaneous physics knowledge -- collision handling, physics simulation, vector arithmetic -- and learned firsthand how computers actually work: memory, caches, CPU cycles, state machines.

    Yet everything I know applies 100% to physics. CAS becomes observation, LRU becomes entropy, hash chains become causality, and ticks become Planck time. This is not analogy. It is equivalence.

    I thought about why.

    The starting point was this: If I were to build the universe as a program, how would I design it? Memory is needed to store state, an operator is needed to change state, an order of operations is needed, and resources must be finite. If infinite resources were allowed, the system would diverge and nothing could exist stably. An atomic operation that reads, compares, and writes state on finite resources. That is CAS. As a programmer, I simply designed the most efficient system possible.

    But when the design was complete and I cross-checked it against existing physics equations, they were all compatible. 118 physics equations, FAIL 0. E=mc squared emerged, the uncertainty principle emerged, black hole entropy emerged. I did not fit physics equations into the design. I designed first, then verified compatibility with physics afterward. I never changed the design for compatibility. All 118 equations fit into the original design as-is.

    This is profoundly interesting. The result of a programmer designing "the most efficient system" exactly matches the laws that physicists discovered through 300 years of experiments.

    Why do they match?

    A programmer's thinking seeks the shortest path. It gravitates toward the shortest and most efficient logical structure under given constraints. Physical phenomena also follow the shortest path. Light travels the minimum-time path per Fermat's principle, particles choose the path where the action S = integral of L dt is minimized per the Principle of Least Action, water flows to the lowest point, and spacetime around a Kerr black hole spirals along geodesics. Nature always selects the most efficient path. So do programmers.

    This is not coincidence. The shape of the universe itself follows the shortest path of logic. There is only one logically possible structure, and the universe chose it. 4-axis orthogonality. Write and evict. Finite resources. CAS. No other structure is logically possible. That is why a programmer's knowledge applies to physics. The reason I could describe physics without studying it is not because I am a genius, but because there is only one place to arrive at. Perhaps, by pursuing logical convergence through CS, I stumbled upon the very principles governing physical phenomena.

    The Banya Framework is evidence of that convergence.

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    delta: change(change) | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition
